<s> QUEEN MARY </s>
<s> ACT I </s>
<s> SCENE I.--ALDGATE RICHLY DECORATED </s>
<s> CROWD </s>
<s> MARSHALMEN </s>
<s> MARSHALMAN </s>
<s> Stand back, keep a clear lane </s>
<s> When will her Majesty pass, sayst thou </s>
<s> why now, even now; wherefore draw back your heads and your horns before I break them, and make what noise you will with your tongues, so it be not treason </s>
<s> Long live Queen Mary, the lawful and legitimate daughter of Harry the Eighth </s>
<s> Shout, knaves </s>
<s> CITIZENS </s>
<s> Long live Queen Mary </s>
<s> FIRST CITIZEN </s>
<s> That's a hard word, legitimate; what does it mean </s>
<s> SECOND CITIZEN </s>
<s> It means a bastard </s>
<s> THIRD CITIZEN </s>
<s> Nay, it means true-born </s>
<s> FIRST CITIZEN </s>
<s> Why, didn't the Parliament make her a bastard </s>
<s> SECOND CITIZEN </s>
<s> No; it was the Lady Elizabeth </s>
<s> THIRD CITIZEN </s>
<s> That was after, man; that was after </s>
<s> FIRST CITIZEN </s>
<s> Then which is the bastard </s>
<s> SECOND CITIZEN </s>
<s> Troth, they be both bastards by Act of Parliament and Council </s>
<s> THIRD CITIZEN </s>
<s> Ay, the Parliament can make every true-born man of us a bastard </s>
<s> Old Nokes, can't it make thee a bastard </s>
<s> thou shouldst know, for thou art as white as three Christmasses </s>
<s> OLD NOKES (_dreamily_) </s>
<s> Who's a-passing </s>
<s> King Edward or King Richard </s>
<s> THIRD CITIZEN </s>
<s> No, old Nokes </s>
<s> OLD NOKES </s>
<s> It's Harry </s>
<s> THIRD CITIZEN </s>
<s> It's Queen Mary </s>
<s> OLD NOKES </s>
<s> The blessed Mary's a-passing </s>
<s> [_Falls on his knees_ </s>
<s> NOKES </s>
<s> Let father alone, my masters </s>
<s> he's past your questioning </s>
<s> THIRD CITIZEN </s>
<s> Answer thou for him, then thou'rt no such cockerel thyself, for thou was born i' the tail end of old Harry the Seventh </s>
<s> NOKES </s>
<s> Eh </s>
<s> that was afore bastard-making began </s>
<s> I was born true man at five in the forenoon i' the tail of old Harry, and so they can't make me a bastard </s>
<s> THIRD CITIZEN </s>
<s> But if Parliament can make the Queen a bastard, why, it follows all the more that they can make thee one, who art fray'd i' the knees, and out at elbow, and bald o' the back, and bursten at the toes, and down at heels </s>
<s> NOKES </s>
<s> I was born of a true man and a ring'd wife, and I can't argue upon it; but I and my old woman 'ud burn upon it, that would we </s>
<s> MARSHALMAN </s>
<s> What are you cackling of bastardy under the Queen's own nose </s>
<s> I'll have you flogg'd and burnt too, by the Rood I will </s>
<s> FIRST CITIZEN </s>
<s> He swears by the Rood </s>
<s> Whew </s>
<s> SECOND CITIZEN </s>
<s> Hark </s>
<s> the trumpets </s>
<s> [_The Procession passes_, MARY _and_ ELIZABETH _riding side by side, and disappears under the gate_ </s>
<s> CITIZENS </s>
<s> Long live Queen Mary </s>
<s> down with all traitors </s>
<s> God save her Grace; and death to Northumberland </s>
<s> [_Exeunt_ </s>
<s> _Manent_ TWO GENTLEMEN </s>
<s> FIRST GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> By God's light a noble creature, right royal </s>
<s> SECOND GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> She looks comelier than ordinary to-day; but to my mind the Lady Elizabeth is the more noble and royal </s>
<s> FIRST GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> I mean the Lady Elizabeth </s>
<s> Did you hear (I have a daughter in her service who reported it) that she met the Queen at Wanstead with five hundred horse, and the Queen (tho' some say they be much divided) took her hand, call'd her sweet sister, and kiss'd not her alone, but all the ladies of her following </s>
<s> SECOND GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> Ay, that was in her hour of joy; there will be plenty to sunder and unsister them again: this Gardiner for one, who is to be made Lord Chancellor, and will pounce like a wild beast out of his cage to worry Cranmer </s>
<s> FIRST GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> And furthermore, my daughter said that when there rose a talk of the late rebellion, she spoke even of Northumberland pitifully, and of the good Lady Jane as a poor innocent child who had but obeyed her father; and furthermore, she said that no one in her time should be burnt for heresy </s>
<s> SECOND GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> Well, sir, I look for happy times </s>
<s> FIRST GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> There is but one thing against them </s>
<s> I know not if you know </s>
<s> SECOND GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> I suppose you touch upon the rumour that Charles, the master of the world, has offer'd her his son Philip, the Pope and the Devil </s>
<s> I trust it is but a rumour </s>
<s> FIRST GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> She is going now to the Tower to loose the prisoners there, and among them Courtenay, to be made Earl of Devon, of royal blood, of splendid feature, whom the council and all her people wish her to marry </s>
<s> May it be so, for we are many of us Catholics, but few Papists, and the Hot Gospellers will go mad upon it </s>
<s> SECOND GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> Was she not betroth'd in her babyhood to the Great Emperor himself </s>
<s> FIRST GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> Ay, but he's too old </s>
<s> SECOND GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> And again to her cousin Reginald Pole, now Cardinal; but I hear that he too is full of aches and broken before his day </s>
<s> FIRST GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> O, the Pope could dispense with his Cardinalate, and his achage, and his breakage, if that were all: will you not follow the procession </s>
<s> SECOND GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> No; I have seen enough for this day </s>
<s> FIRST GENTLEMAN </s>
<s> Well, I shall follow; if I can get near enough I shall judge with my own eyes whether her Grace incline to this splendid scion of Plantagenet </s>
<s> [_Exeunt_ </s>
<s> SCENE II.--A ROOM IN LAMBETH PALACE </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> To Strasburg, Antwerp, Frankfort, Zurich, Worms, Geneva, Basle--our Bishops from their sees Or fled, they say, or flying--Poinet, Barlow, Bale, Scory, Coverdale; besides the Deans Of Christchurch, Durham, Exeter, and Wells-- Ailmer and Bullingham, and hundreds more; So they report: I shall be left alone </s>
<s> No: Hooper, Ridley, Latimer will not fly </s>
<s> _Enter_ PETER MARTYR </s>
<s> PETER MARTYR </s>
<s> Fly, Cranmer </s>
<s> were there nothing else, your name Stands first of those who sign'd the Letters Patent That gave her royal crown to Lady Jane </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> Stand first it may, but it was written last: Those that are now her Privy Council, sign'd Before me: nay, the Judges had pronounced That our young Edward might bequeath the crown Of England, putting by his father's will </s>
<s> Yet I stood out, till Edward sent for me </s>
<s> The wan boy-king, with his fast-fading eyes Fixt hard on mine, his frail transparent hand, Damp with the sweat of death, and griping mine, Whisper'd me, if I loved him, not to yield His Church of England to the Papal wolf And Mary; then I could no more--I sign'd </s>
<s> Nay, for bare shame of inconsistency, She cannot pass her traitor council by, To make me headless </s>
<s> PETER MARTYR </s>
<s> That might be forgiven </s>
<s> I tell you, fly, my Lord </s>
<s> You do not own The bodily presence in the Eucharist, Their wafer and perpetual sacrifice: Your creed will be your death </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> Step after step, Thro' many voices crying right and left, Have I climb'd back into the primal church, And stand within the porch, and Christ with me: My flight were such a scandal to the faith, The downfall of so many simple souls, I dare not leave my post </s>
<s> PETER MARTYR </s>
<s> But you divorced Queen Catharine and her father; hence, her hate Will burn till you are burn'd </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> I cannot help it </s>
<s> The Canonists and Schoolmen were with me </s>
<s> 'Thou shalt not wed thy brother's wife'.--'Tis written, 'They shall be childless' </s>
<s> True, Mary was born, But France would not accept her for a bride As being born from incest; and this wrought Upon the king; and child by child, you know, Were momentary sparkles out as quick Almost as kindled; and he brought his doubts And fears to me </s>
<s> Peter, I'll swear for him He _did_ believe the bond incestuous </s>
<s> But wherefore am I trenching on the time That should already have seen your steps a mile From me and Lambeth </s>
<s> God be with you </s>
<s> Go </s>
<s> PETER MARTYR </s>
<s> Ah, but how fierce a letter you wrote against Their superstition when they slander'd you For setting up a mass at Canterbury To please the Queen </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> It was a wheedling monk Set up the mass </s>
<s> PETER MARTYR </s>
<s> I know it, my good Lord </s>
<s> But you so bubbled over with hot terms Of Satan, liars, blasphemy, Antichrist, She never will forgive you </s>
<s> Fly, my Lord, fly </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> I wrote it, and God grant me power to burn </s>
<s> PETER MARTYR </s>
<s> They have given me a safe conduct: for all that I dare not stay </s>
<s> I fear, I fear, I see you, Dear friend, for the last time; farewell, and fly </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> Fly and farewell, and let me die the death </s>
<s> [_Exit_ PETER MARTYR </s>
<s> _Enter_ OLD SERVANT </s>
<s> O, kind and gentle master, the Queen's Officers Are here in force to take you to the Tower </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> Ay, gentle friend, admit them </s>
<s> I will go </s>
<s> I thank my God it is too late to fly </s>
<s> [_Exeunt_ </s>
<s> SCENE III.--ST </s>
<s> PAUL'S CROSS </s>
<s> FATHER BOURNE _in the pulpit_ </s>
<s> A CROWD </s>
<s> MARCHIONESS OF EXETER, COURTENAY </s>
<s> _The_ SIEUR DE NOAILLES _and his man_ ROGER _in front of the stage </s>
<s> Hubbub_ </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> Hast thou let fall those papers in the palace </s>
<s> ROGER </s>
<s> Ay, sir </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> 'There will be no peace for Mary till Elizabeth lose her head' </s>
<s> ROGER </s>
<s> Ay, sir </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> And the other, 'Long live Elizabeth the Queen' </s>
<s> ROGER </s>
<s> Ay, sir; she needs must tread upon them </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> Well </s>
<s> These beastly swine make such a grunting here, I cannot catch what Father Bourne is saying </s>
<s> ROGER </s>
<s> Quiet a moment, my masters; hear what the shaveling has to say for himself </s>
<s> CROWD </s>
<s> Hush--hear </s>
<s> BOURNE.--and so this unhappy land, long divided in itself, and sever'd from the faith, will return into the one true fold, seeing that our gracious Virgin Queen hath---- CROWD </s>
<s> No pope </s>
<s> no pope </s>
<s> ROGER (_to those about him, mimicking_ BOURNE).--hath sent for the holy legate of the holy father the Pope, Cardinal Pole, to give us all that holy absolution which---- FIRST CITIZEN </s>
<s> Old Bourne to the life </s>
<s> SECOND CITIZEN </s>
<s> Holy absolution </s>
<s> holy Inquisition </s>
<s> THIRD CITIZEN </s>
<s> Down with the Papist </s>
<s> [_Hubbub_ </s>
<s> BOURNE.--and now that your good bishop, Bonner, who hath lain so long under bonds for the faith-- [_Hubbub_ </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> Friend Roger, steal thou in among the crowd, And get the swine to shout Elizabeth </s>
<s> Yon gray old Gospeller, sour as midwinter, Begin with him </s>
<s> ROGER (_goes_) </s>
<s> By the mass, old friend, we'll have no pope here while the Lady Elizabeth lives </s>
<s> GOSPELLER </s>
<s> Art thou of the true faith, fellow, that swearest by the mass </s>
<s> ROGER </s>
<s> Ay, that am I, new converted, but the old leaven sticks to my tongue yet </s>
<s> FIRST CITIZEN </s>
<s> He says right; by the mass we'll have no mass here </s>
<s> VOICES OF THE CROWD </s>
<s> Peace </s>
<s> hear him; let his own words damn the Papist </s>
<s> From thine own mouth I judge thee--tear him down </s>
<s> BOURNE.--and since our Gracious Queen, let me call her our second Virgin Mary, hath begun to re-edify the true temple----, FIRST CITIZEN </s>
<s> Virgin Mary </s>
<s> we'll have no virgins here--we'll have the Lady Elizabeth </s>
<s> [_Swords are drawn, a knife is hurled and sticks in the pulpit </s>
<s> The mob throng to the pulpit stairs_ </s>
<s> MARCHIONESS OF EXETER </s>
<s> Son Courtenay, wilt thou see the holy father Murdered before thy face </s>
<s> up, son, and save him </s>
<s> They love thee, and thou canst not come to harm </s>
<s> COURTENAY (_in the pulpit_) </s>
<s> Shame, shame, my masters </s>
<s> are you English-born, And set yourselves by hundreds against one </s>
<s> CROWD </s>
<s> A Courtenay </s>
<s> a Courtenay </s>
<s> [_A train of Spanish servants crosses at the back of the stage_ </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> These birds of passage come before their time: Stave off the crowd upon the Spaniard there </s>
<s> ROGER </s>
<s> My masters, yonder's fatter game for you Than this old gaping gurgoyle: look you there-- The Prince of Spain coming to wed our Queen </s>
<s> After him, boys </s>
<s> and pelt him from the city </s>
<s> [_They seize stones and follow the Spaniards </s>
<s> Exeunt on the other side_ MARCHIONESS OF EXETER _and_ ATTENDANTS </s>
<s> NOAILLES (_to_ ROGER) </s>
<s> Stand from me </s>
<s> If Elizabeth lose her head-- That makes for France </s>
<s> And if her people, anger'd thereupon, Arise against her and dethrone the Queen-- That makes for France </s>
<s> And if I breed confusion anyway-- That makes for France </s>
<s> Good-day, my Lord of Devon; A bold heart yours to beard that raging mob </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> My mother said, Go up; and up I went </s>
<s> I knew they would not do me any wrong, For I am mighty popular with them, Noailles </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> You look'd a king </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> Why not </s>
<s> I am king's blood </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> And in the whirl of change may come to be one </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> Ah </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> But does your gracious Queen entreat you kinglike </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> 'Fore God, I think she entreats me like a child </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> You've but a dull life in this maiden court, I fear, my Lord </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> A life of nods and yawns </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> So you would honour my poor house to-night, We might enliven you </s>
<s> Divers honest fellows, The Duke of Suffolk lately freed from prison, Sir Peter Carew and Sir Thomas Wyatt, Sir Thomas Stafford, and some more--we play </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> At what </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> The Game of Chess </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> The Game of Chess </s>
<s> I can play well, and I shall beat you there </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> Ay, but we play with Henry, King of France, And certain of his court </s>
<s> His Highness makes his moves across the Channel, We answer him with ours, and there are messengers That go between us </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> Why, such a game, sir, were whole years a playing </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> Nay; not so long I trust </s>
<s> That all depends Upon the skill and swiftness of the players </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> The King is skilful at it </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> Very, my Lord </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> And the stakes high </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> But not beyond your means </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> Well, I'm the first of players, I shall win </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> With our advice and in our company, And so you well attend to the king's moves, I think you may </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> When do you meet </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> To-night </s>
<s> COURTENAY (_aside_) </s>
<s> I will be there; the fellow's at his tricks-- Deep--I shall fathom him </s>
<s> (_Aloud_) Good morning, Noailles </s>
<s> [_Exit_ COURTENAY </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> Good-day, my Lord </s>
<s> Strange game of chess </s>
<s> a King That with her own pawns plays against a Queen, Whose play is all to find herself a King </s>
<s> Ay; but this fine blue-blooded Courtenay seems Too princely for a pawn </s>
<s> Call him a Knight, That, with an ass's, not a horse's head, Skips every way, from levity or from fear </s>
<s> Well, we shall use him somehow, so that Gardiner And Simon Renard spy not out our game Too early </s>
<s> Roger, thinkest thou that anyone Suspected thee to be my man </s>
<s> ROGER </s>
<s> Not one, sir </s>
<s> NOAILLES </s>
<s> No </s>
<s> the disguise was perfect </s>
<s> Let's away </s>
<s> [_Exeunt_ </s>
<s> SCENE IV.--LONDON </s>
<s> A ROOM IN THE PALACE </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> _Enter_ COURTENAY </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> So yet am I, Unless my friends and mirrors lie to me, A goodlier-looking fellow than this Philip </s>
<s> Pah </s>
<s> The Queen is ill advised: shall I turn traitor </s>
<s> They've almost talked me into it: yet the word Affrights me somewhat: to be such a one As Harry Bolingbroke hath a lure in it </s>
<s> Good now, my Lady Queen, tho' by your age, And by your looks you are not worth the having, Yet by your crown you are </s>
<s> [_Seeing_ ELIZABETH </s>
<s> The Princess there </s>
<s> If I tried her and la--she's amorous </s>
<s> Have we not heard of her in Edward's time, Her freaks and frolics with the late Lord Admiral </s>
<s> I do believe she'd yield </s>
<s> I should be still A party in the state; and then, who knows-- ELIZABETH </s>
<s> What are you musing on, my Lord of Devon </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> Has not the Queen-- ELIZABETH </s>
<s> Done what, Sir </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> --made you follow The Lady Suffolk and the Lady Lennox?-- You, The heir presumptive </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> Why do you ask </s>
<s> you know it </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> You needs must bear it hardly </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> No, indeed </s>
<s> I am utterly submissive to the Queen </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> Well, I was musing upon that; the Queen Is both my foe and yours: we should be friends </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> My Lord, the hatred of another to us Is no true bond of friendship </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> Might it not Be the rough preface of some closer bond </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> My Lord, you late were loosed from out the Tower, Where, like a butterfly in a chrysalis, You spent your life; that broken, out you flutter Thro' the new world, go zigzag, now would settle Upon this flower, now that; but all things here At court are known; you have solicited The Queen, and been rejected </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> Flower, she </s>
<s> Half faded </s>
<s> but you, cousin, are fresh and sweet As the first flower no bee has ever tried </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> Are you the bee to try me </s>
<s> why, but now I called you butterfly </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> You did me wrong, I love not to be called a butterfly: Why do you call me butterfly </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> Why do you go so gay then </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> Velvet and gold </s>
<s> This dress was made me as the Earl of Devon To take my seat in; looks it not right royal </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> So royal that the Queen forbad you wearing it </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> I wear it then to spite her </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> My Lord, my Lord; I see you in the Tower again </s>
<s> Her Majesty Hears you affect the Prince--prelates kneel to you.-- COURTENAY </s>
<s> I am the noblest blood in Europe, Madam, A Courtenay of Devon, and her cousin </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> She hears you make your boast that after all She means to wed you </s>
<s> Folly, my good Lord </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> How folly </s>
<s> a great party in the state Wills me to wed her </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> Failing her, my Lord, Doth not as great a party in the state Will you to wed me </s>
<s> COURTENAY </s>
<s> Even so, fair lady </s>

<s> SCENE V.--A ROOM IN THE PALACE </s>
<s> MARY _with_ PHILIP'S _miniature_ </s>

<s> ALICE </s>

<s> What wast thou saying of this Lady Jane, Now in the Tower </s>

<s> Why, Madam, she was passing Some chapel down in Essex, and with her Lady Anne Wharton, and the Lady Anne Bow'd to the Pyx; but Lady Jane stood up Stiff as the very backbone of heresy </s>

<s> Paget is for him--for to wed with Spain Would treble England--Gardiner is against him; The Council, people, Parliament against him; But I will have him </s>

<s> ACT II SCENE I.--ALINGTON CASTLE </s>
<s> SIR THOMAS WYATT </s>
<s> I do not hear from Carew or the Duke Of Suffolk, and till then I should not move </s>
<s> The Duke hath gone to Leicester; Carew stirs In Devon: that fine porcelain Courtenay, Save that he fears he might be crack'd in using, (I have known a semi-madman in my time So fancy-ridd'n) should be in Devon too </s>
<s> _Enter_ WILLIAM </s>
<s> News abroad, William </s>

<s> WILLIAM </s>

<s> WYATT </s>

<s> The sire begets Not half his likeness in the son </s>
<s> I fail Where he was fullest: yet--to write it down </s>
<s> [_He writes_ </s>
<s> _Re-enter_ WILLIAM </s>
<s> WILLIAM </s>
<s> There _is_ news, there _is_ news, and no call for sonnet-sorting now, nor for sonnet-making either, but ten thousand men on Penenden Heath all calling after your worship, and your worship's name heard into Maidstone market, and your worship the first man in Kent and Christendom, for the Queen's down, and the world's up, and your worship a-top of it </s>
<s> WYATT </s>
<s> Inverted Aesop--mountain out of mouse </s>
<s> Say for ten thousand ten--and pothouse knaves, Brain-dizzied with a draught of morning ale </s>

<s> They roar for you On Penenden Heath, a thousand of them--more-- All arm'd, waiting a leader; there's no glory Like his who saves his country: and you sit Sing-songing here; but, if I'm any judge, By God, you are as poor a poet, Wyatt, As a good soldier </s>

<s> Men of Kent; England of England; you that have kept your old customs upright, while all the rest of England bow'd theirs to the Norman, the cause that hath brought us together is not the cause of a county or a shire, but of this England, in whose crown our Kent is the fairest jewel </s>

<s> I know Spain </s>

<s> SCENE II.--GUILDHALL </s>
<s> SIR THOMAS WHITE (The Lord Mayor), LORD WILLIAM HOWARD, SIR RALPH BAGENHALL, ALDERMEN _and_ CITIZENS </s>
<s> WHITE </s>
<s> I trust the Queen comes hither with her guards </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> Ay, all in arms </s>

<s> You know that after The Captain Brett, who went with your train bands To fight with Wyatt, had gone over to him With all his men, the Queen in that distress Sent Cornwallis and Hastings to the traitor, Feigning to treat with him about her marriage-- Know too what Wyatt said </s>
<s> WHITE </s>

<s> WHITE </s>
<s> How look'd the city When now you past it </s>
<s> Quiet </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> Like our Council, Your city is divided </s>
<s> As we past, Some hail'd, some hiss'd us </s>
<s> There were citizens Stood each before his shut-up booth, and look'd As grim and grave as from a funeral </s>
<s> And here a knot of ruffians all in rags, With execrating execrable eyes, Glared at the citizen </s>
<s> Here was a young mother, Her face on flame, her red hair all blown back, She shrilling 'Wyatt,' while the boy she held Mimick'd and piped her 'Wyatt,' as red as she In hair and cheek; and almost elbowing her, So close they stood, another, mute as death, And white as her own milk; her babe in arms Had felt the faltering of his mother's heart, And look'd as bloodless </s>
<s> Here a pious Catholic, Mumbling and mixing up in his scared prayers Heaven and earth's Maries; over his bow'd shoulder Scowl'd that world-hated and world-hating beast, A haggard Anabaptist </s>
<s> Many such groups </s>
<s> The names of Wyatt, Elizabeth, Courtenay, Nay the Queen's right to reign--'fore God, the rogues-- Were freely buzzed among them </s>
<s> So I say Your city is divided, and I fear One scruple, this or that way, of success Would turn it thither </s>
<s> Wherefore now the Queen In this low pulse and palsy of the state, Bad me to tell you that she counts on you And on myself as her two hands; on you, In your own city, as her right, my Lord, For you are loyal </s>

<s> Am I Thomas White </s>

<s> WHITE </s>
<s> God send her well; Here comes her Royal Grace </s>
<s> _Enter_ GUARDS, MARY _and_ GARDINER </s>
<s> SIR THOMAS WHITE _leads her to a raised seat on the dais_ </s>
<s> WHITE </s>
<s> I, the Lord Mayor, and these our companies And guilds of London, gathered here, beseech Your Highness to accept our lowliest thanks For your most princely presence; and we pray That we, your true and loyal citizens, From your own royal lips, at once may know The wherefore of this coming, and so learn Your royal will, and do it.--I, Lord Mayor Of London, and our guilds and companies </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> In mine own person am I come to you, To tell you what indeed ye see and know, How traitorously these rebels out of Kent Have made strong head against ourselves and you </s>
<s> They would not have me wed the Prince of Spain: That was their pretext--so they spake at first-- But we sent divers of our Council to them, And by their answers to the question ask'd, It doth appear this marriage is the least Of all their quarrel </s>
<s> They have betrayed the treason of their hearts: Seek to possess our person, hold our Tower, Place and displace our councillors, and use Both us and them according as they will </s>
<s> Now what I am ye know right well--your Queen; To whom, when I was wedded to the realm And the realm's laws (the spousal ring whereof, Not ever to be laid aside, I wear Upon this finger), ye did promise full Allegiance and obedience to the death </s>
<s> Ye know my father was the rightful heir Of England, and his right came down to me Corroborate by your acts of Parliament: And as ye were most loving unto him, So doubtless will ye show yourselves to me </s>
<s> Wherefore, ye will not brook that anyone Should seize our person, occupy our state, More specially a traitor so presumptuous As this same Wyatt, who hath tamper'd with A public ignorance, and, under colour Of such a cause as hath no colour, seeks To bend the laws to his own will, and yield Full scope to persons rascal and forlorn, To make free spoil and havock of your goods </s>
<s> Now as your Prince, I say, I, that was never mother, cannot tell How mothers love their children; yet, methinks, A prince as naturally may love his people As these their children; and be sure your Queen So loves you, and so loving, needs must deem This love by you return'd as heartily; And thro' this common knot and bond of love, Doubt not they will be speedily overthrown </s>
<s> As to this marriage, ye shall understand We made thereto no treaty of ourselves, And set no foot theretoward unadvised Of all our Privy Council; furthermore, This marriage had the assent of those to whom The king, my father, did commit his trust; Who not alone esteem'd it honourable, But for the wealth and glory of our realm, And all our loving subjects, most expedient </s>
<s> As to myself, I am not so set on wedlock as to choose But where I list, nor yet so amorous That I must needs be husbanded; I thank God, I have lived a virgin, and I noway doubt But that with God's grace, I can live so still </s>
<s> Yet if it might please God that I should leave Some fruit of mine own body after me, To be your king, ye would rejoice thereat, And it would be your comfort, as I trust; And truly, if I either thought or knew This marriage should bring loss or danger to you, My subjects, or impair in any way This royal state of England, I would never Consent thereto, nor marry while I live; Moreover, if this marriage should not seem, Before our own High Court of Parliament, To be of rich advantage to our realm, We will refrain, and not alone from this, Likewise from any other, out of which Looms the least chance of peril to our realm </s>
<s> Wherefore be bold, and with your lawful Prince Stand fast against our enemies and yours, And fear them not </s>
<s> I fear them not </s>
<s> My Lord, I leave Lord William Howard in your city, To guard and keep you whole and safe from all The spoil and sackage aim'd at by these rebels, Who mouth and foam against the Prince of Spain </s>

<s> Courage, sir, _That_ makes or man or woman look their goodliest </s>
<s> Die like the torn fox dumb, but never whine Like that poor heart, Northumberland, at the block </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> The man had children, and he whined for those </s>
<s> Methinks most men are but poor-hearted, else Should we so doat on courage, were it commoner </s>
<s> The Queen stands up, and speaks for her own self; And all men cry, She is queenly, she is goodly </s>
<s> Yet she's no goodlier; tho' my Lord Mayor here, By his own rule, he hath been so bold to-day, Should look more goodly than the rest of us </s>
<s> WHITE </s>
<s> Goodly </s>
<s> I feel most goodly heart and hand, And strong to throw ten Wyatts and all Kent </s>
<s> Ha </s>
<s> ha </s>
<s> sir; but you jest; I love it: a jest In time of danger shows the pulses even </s>
<s> Be merry </s>
<s> yet, Sir Ralph, you look but sad </s>
<s> I dare avouch you'd stand up for yourself, Tho' all the world should bay like winter wolves </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> Who knows </s>
<s> the man is proven by the hour </s>
<s> WHITE </s>
<s> The man should make the hour, not this the man; And Thomas White will prove this Thomas Wyatt, And he will prove an Iden to this Cade, And he will play the Walworth to this Wat; Come, sirs, we prate; hence all--gather your men-- Myself must bustle </s>
<s> Wyatt comes to Southwark; I'll have the drawbridge hewn into the Thames, And see the citizens arm'd </s>

<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> One of much outdoor bluster </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> For all that, Most honest, brave, and skilful; and his wealth A fountain of perennial alms--his fault So thoroughly to believe in his own self </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> Yet thoroughly to believe in one's own self, So one's own self be thorough, were to do Great things, my Lord </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> It may be </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> I have heard One of your Council fleer and jeer at him </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> The nursery-cocker'd child will jeer at aught That may seem strange beyond his nursery </s>
<s> The statesman that shall jeer and fleer at men, Makes enemies for himself and for his king; And if he jeer not seeing the true man Behind his folly, he is thrice the fool; And if he see the man and still will jeer, He is child and fool, and traitor to the State </s>
<s> Who is he </s>
<s> let me shun him </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> Nay, my Lord, He is damn'd enough already </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> I must set The guard at Ludgate </s>

<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> 'Who knows' </s>
<s> I am for England </s>

<s> SCENE III.--LONDON BRIDGE </s>
<s> _Enter_ SIR THOMAS WYATT _and_ BRETT </s>

<s> ACT III </s>
<s> SCENE I.--THE CONDUIT IN GRACECHURCH, _Painted with the Nine Worthies, among them King Henry VIII </s>
<s> holding a book, on it inscribed_ 'Verbum Dei' </s>
<s> _Enter_ SIR RALPH BAGENHALL _and_ SIR THOMAS STAFFORD </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> A hundred here and hundreds hang'd in Kent </s>
<s> The tigress had unsheath'd her nails at last, And Renard and the Chancellor sharpen'd them </s>
<s> In every London street a gibbet stood </s>
<s> They are down to-day </s>
<s> Here by this house was one; The traitor husband dangled at the door, And when the traitor wife came out for bread To still the petty treason therewithin, Her cap would brush his heels </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> It is Sir Ralph, And muttering to himself as heretofore </s>
<s> Sir, see you aught up yonder </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> I miss something </s>
<s> The tree that only bears dead fruit is gone </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> What tree, sir </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> Well, the tree in Virgil, sir, That bears not its own apples </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> What </s>
<s> the gallows </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> Sir, this dead fruit was ripening overmuch, And had to be removed lest living Spain Should sicken at dead England </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> Not so dead, But that a shock may rouse her </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> I believe Sir Thomas Stafford </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> I am ill disguised </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> Well, are you not in peril here </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> I think so </s>
<s> I came to feel the pulse of England, whether It beats hard at this marriage </s>
<s> Did you see it </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> Stafford, I am a sad man and a serious </s>
<s> Far liefer had I in my country hall Been reading some old book, with mine old hound Couch'd at my hearth, and mine old flask of wine Beside me, than have seen it: yet I saw it </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> Good, was it splendid </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> Ay, if Dukes, and Earls, And Counts, and sixty Spanish cavaliers, Some six or seven Bishops, diamonds, pearls, That royal commonplace too, cloth of gold, Could make it so </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> And what was Mary's dress </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> Good faith, I was too sorry for the woman To mark the dress </s>
<s> She wore red shoes </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> Red shoes </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> Scarlet, as if her feet were wash'd in blood, As if she had waded in it </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> Were your eyes So bashful that you look'd no higher </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> A diamond, And Philip's gift, as proof of Philip's love, Who hath not any for any,--tho' a true one, Blazed false upon her heart </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> But this proud Prince-- BAGENHALL </s>
<s> Nay, he is King, you know, the King of Naples </s>
<s> The father ceded Naples, that the son Being a King, might wed a Queen--O he Flamed in brocade--white satin his trunk-hose, Inwrought with silver,--on his neck a collar, Gold, thick with diamonds; hanging down from this The Golden Fleece--and round his knee, misplaced, Our English Garter, studded with great emeralds, Rubies, I know not what </s>
<s> Have you had enough Of all this gear </s>
<s> STAFFORD </s>
<s> Ay, since you hate the telling it </s>

<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> No fairer for her jewels </s>
<s> And I could see that as the new-made couple Came from the Minster, moving side by side Beneath one canopy, ever and anon She cast on him a vassal smile of love, Which Philip with a glance of some distaste, Or so methought, return'd </s>
<s> I may be wrong, sir </s>

<s> I think with you </s>

<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> France </s>
<s> We have once had half of France, and hurl'd our battles Into the heart of Spain; but England now Is but a ball chuck'd between France and Spain, His in whose hand she drops; Harry of Bolingbroke Had holpen Richard's tottering throne to stand, Could Harry have foreseen that all our nobles Would perish on the civil slaughter-field, And leave the people naked to the crown, And the crown naked to the people; the crown Female, too </s>
<s> Sir, no woman's regimen Can save us </s>
<s> We are fallen, and as I think, Never to rise again </s>

<s> SCENE II.--ROOM IN WHITEHALL PALACE </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> _Enter_ PHILIP _and_ CARDINAL POLE </s>

<s> MARY </s>
<s> Loyal and royal cousin, humblest thanks </s>
<s> Had you a pleasant voyage up the river </s>
<s> POLE </s>
<s> We had your royal barge, and that same chair, Or rather throne of purple, on the deck </s>
<s> Our silver cross sparkled before the prow, The ripples twinkled at their diamond-dance, The boats that follow'd, were as glowing-gay As regal gardens; and your flocks of swans, As fair and white as angels; and your shores Wore in mine eyes the green of Paradise </s>
<s> My foreign friends, who dream'd us blanketed In ever-closing fog, were much amazed To find as fair a sun as might have flash'd Upon their lake of Garda, fire the Thames; Our voyage by sea was all but miracle; And here the river flowing from the sea, Not toward it (for they thought not of our tides), Seem'd as a happy miracle to make glide-- In quiet--home your banish'd countryman </s>

<s> Thou hast disgraced me and attainted me, And mark'd me ev'n as Cain, and I return As Peter, but to bless thee: make me well' </s>

<s> SCENE III.--GREAT HALL IN WHITEHALL </s>
<s> _At the far end a dais </s>
<s> On this three chairs, two under one canopy for_ MARY _and_ PHILIP, _another on the right of these for_ POLE </s>
<s> _Under the dais on_ POLE'S _side, ranged along the wall, sit all the Spiritual Peers, and along the wall opposite, all the Temporal </s>
<s> The Commons on cross benches in front, a line of approach to the dais between them </s>
<s> In the foreground_, SIR RALPH BAGENHALL _and other Members of the Commons_ </s>
<s> FIRST MEMBER </s>
<s> St </s>
<s> Andrew's day; sit close, sit close, we are friends </s>
<s> Is reconciled the word </s>
<s> the Pope again </s>
<s> It must be thus; and yet, cocksbody </s>
<s> how strange That Gardiner, once so one with all of us Against this foreign marriage, should have yielded So utterly!--strange </s>
<s> but stranger still that he, So fierce against the Headship of the Pope, Should play the second actor in this pageant That brings him in; such a cameleon he </s>
<s> SECOND MEMBER </s>
<s> This Gardiner turn'd his coat in Henry's time; The serpent that hath slough'd will slough again </s>
<s> THIRD MEMBER </s>
<s> Tut, then we all are serpents </s>
<s> SECOND MEMBER </s>
<s> Speak for yourself </s>
<s> THIRD MEMBER </s>
<s> Ay, and for Gardiner </s>
<s> being English citizen, How should he bear a bridegroom out of Spain </s>
<s> The Queen would have him </s>
<s> being English churchman How should he bear the headship of the Pope </s>
<s> The Queen would have it </s>
<s> Statesmen that are wise Shape a necessity, as a sculptor clay, To their own model </s>
<s> SECOND MEMBER </s>
<s> Statesmen that are wise Take truth herself for model </s>
<s> What say you </s>
<s> [_To_ SIR RALPH BAGENHALL </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> We talk and talk </s>
<s> FIRST MEMBER </s>
<s> Ay, and what use to talk </s>
<s> Philip's no sudden alien--the Queen's husband, He's here, and king, or will be--yet cocksbody </s>
<s> So hated here </s>
<s> I watch'd a hive of late; My seven-years' friend was with me, my young boy; Out crept a wasp, with half the swarm behind </s>
<s> 'Philip' </s>
<s> says he </s>
<s> I had to cuff the rogue For infant treason </s>
<s> THIRD MEMBER </s>
<s> But they say that bees, If any creeping life invade their hive Too gross to be thrust out, will build him round, And bind him in from harming of their combs </s>
<s> And Philip by these articles is bound From stirring hand or foot to wrong the realm </s>
<s> SECOND MEMBER </s>
<s> By bonds of beeswax, like your creeping thing; But your wise bees had stung him first to death </s>
<s> THIRD MEMBER </s>
<s> Hush, hush </s>
<s> You wrong the Chancellor: the clauses added To that same treaty which the emperor sent us Were mainly Gardiner's: that no foreigner Hold office in the household, fleet, forts, army; That if the Queen should die without a child, The bond between the kingdoms be dissolved; That Philip should not mix us any way With his French wars-- SECOND MEMBER </s>
<s> Ay, ay, but what security, Good sir, for this, if Philip---- THIRD MEMBER </s>
<s> Peace--the Queen, Philip, and Pole </s>
<s> [_All rise, and stand_ </s>
<s> _Enter_ MARY, PHILIP, _and_ POLE </s>
<s> [GARDINER _conducts them to the three chairs of state_ </s>
<s> PHILIP _sits on the_ QUEEN'S _left_, POLE _on her right_ </s>
<s> GARDINER </s>
<s> Our short-lived sun, before his winter plunge, Laughs at the last red leaf, and Andrew's Day </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> Should not this day be held in after years More solemn than of old </s>
<s> PHILIP </s>
<s> Madam, my wish Echoes your Majesty's </s>
<s> POLE </s>
<s> It shall be so </s>
<s> GARDINER </s>
<s> Mine echoes both your Graces'; (_aside_) but the Pope-- Can we not have the Catholic church as well Without as with the Italian </s>
<s> if we cannot, Why then the Pope </s>
<s> My lords of the upper house, And ye, my masters, of the lower house, Do ye stand fast by that which ye resolved </s>
<s> VOICES </s>
<s> We do </s>
<s> GARDINER </s>
<s> And be you all one mind to supplicate The Legate here for pardon, and acknowledge The primacy of the Pope </s>
<s> VOICES </s>
<s> We are all one mind </s>
<s> GARDINER </s>
<s> Then must I play the vassal to this Pole </s>
<s> [_Aside_ </s>
<s> [_He draws a paper from under his robes and presents it to the_ KING _and_ QUEEN, _who look through it and return it to him; then ascends a tribune, and reads_ </s>
<s> We, the Lords Spiritual and Temporal, And Commons here in Parliament assembled, Presenting the whole body of this realm Of England, and dominions of the same, Do make most humble suit unto your Majesties, In our own name and that of all the state, That by your gracious means and intercession Our supplication be exhibited To the Lord Cardinal Pole, sent here as Legate From our most Holy Father Julius, Pope, And from the Apostolic see of Rome; And do declare our penitence and grief For our long schism and disobedience, Either in making laws and ordinances Against the Holy Father's primacy, Or else by doing or by speaking aught Which might impugn or prejudice the same; By this our supplication promising, As well for our own selves as all the realm, That now we be and ever shall be quick, Under and with your Majesties' authorities, To do to the utmost all that in us lies Towards the abrogation and repeal Of all such laws and ordinances made; Whereon we humbly pray your Majesties, As persons undefiled with our offence, So to set forth this humble suit of ours That we the rather by your intercession May from the Apostolic see obtain, Thro' this most reverend Father, absolution, And full release from danger of all censures Of Holy Church that we be fall'n into, So that we may, as children penitent, Be once again received into the bosom And unity of Universal Church; And that this noble realm thro' after years May in this unity and obedience Unto the holy see and reigning Pope Serve God and both your Majesties </s>
<s> VOICES </s>
<s> Amen </s>
<s> [_All sit </s>
<s> [He again presents the petition to the_ KING _and_ QUEEN, _who hand it reverentially to_ POLE </s>
<s> POLE (_sitting_) </s>
<s> This is the loveliest day that ever smiled On England </s>
<s> All her breath should, incenselike, Rise to the heavens in grateful praise of Him Who now recalls her to His ancient fold </s>
<s> Lo </s>
<s> once again God to this realm hath given A token of His more especial Grace; For as this people were the first of all The islands call'd into the dawning church Out of the dead, deep night of heathendom, So now are these the first whom God hath given Grace to repent and sorrow for their schism; And if your penitence be not mockery, Oh how the blessed angels who rejoice Over one saved do triumph at this hour In the reborn salvation of a land So noble </s>
<s> [_A pause_ </s>
<s> For ourselves we do protest That our commission is to heal, not harm; We come not to condemn, but reconcile; We come not to compel, but call again; We come not to destroy, but edify; Nor yet to question things already done; These are forgiven--matters of the past-- And range with jetsam and with offal thrown Into the blind sea of forgetfulness </s>
<s> [_A pause_ </s>
<s> Ye have reversed the attainder laid on us By him who sack'd the house of God; and we, Amplier than any field on our poor earth Can render thanks in fruit for being sown, Do here and now repay you sixty-fold, A hundred, yea, a thousand thousand-fold, With heaven for earth </s>
<s> [_Rising and stretching forth his hands </s>
<s> All kneel but_ SIR RALPH BAGENHALL, _who rises and remains standing_ </s>
<s> The Lord who hath redeem'd us With His own blood, and wash'd us from our sins, To purchase for Himself a stainless bride; He, whom the Father hath appointed Head Of all his church, He by His mercy absolve you </s>

<s> And we by that authority Apostolic, Given unto us, his Legate, by the Pope, Our Lord and Holy Father, Julius, God's Vicar and Vicegerent upon earth, Do here absolve you and deliver you And every one of you, and all the realm And its dominions from all heresy, All schism, and from all and every censure, Judgment, and pain accruing thereupon; And also we restore you to the bosom And unity of Universal Church </s>

<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> We strove against the papacy from the first, In William's time, in our first Edward's time, And in my master Henry's time; but now, The unity of Universal Church, Mary would have it; and this Gardiner follows; The unity of Universal Hell, Philip would have it; and this Gardiner follows </s>

<s> ELIZABETH </s>

<s> Help me: what think you, Is it life or death </s>
<s> BEDINGFIELD </s>
<s> I thought not on my boots; The devil take all boots were ever made Since man went barefoot </s>
<s> See, I lay it here, For I will come no nearer to your Grace; [_Laying down the letter_ </s>
<s> And, whether it bring you bitter news or sweet, And God hath given your Grace a nose, or not, I'll help you, if I may </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> Your pardon, then; It is the heat and narrowness of the cage That makes the captive testy; with free wing The world were all one Araby </s>
<s> Leave me now, Will you, companion to myself, sir </s>
<s> BEDINGFIELD </s>
<s> Will I </s>
<s> With most exceeding willingness, I will; You know I never come till I be call'd </s>
<s> [_Exit_ </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> It lies there folded: is there venom in it </s>
<s> A snake--and if I touch it, it may sting </s>
<s> Come, come, the worst </s>
<s> Best wisdom is to know the worst at once </s>
<s> [_Reads:_ 'It is the King's wish, that you should wed Prince Philibert of Savoy </s>
<s> You are to come to Court on the instant; and think of this in your coming </s>
<s> 'MARY THE QUEEN' </s>
<s> Think I have many thoughts; I think there may be birdlime here for me; I think they fain would have me from the realm; I think the Queen may never bear a child; I think that I may be some time the Queen, Then, Queen indeed: no foreign prince or priest Should fill my throne, myself upon the steps </s>
<s> I think I will not marry anyone, Specially not this landless Philibert Of Savoy; but, if Philip menace me, I think that I will play with Philibert, As once the Holy Father did with mine, Before my father married my good mother,-- For fear of Spain </s>
<s> _Enter_ LADY </s>
<s> LADY </s>
<s> O Lord </s>
<s> your Grace, your Grace, I feel so happy: it seems that we shall fly These bald, blank fields, and dance into the sun That shines on princes </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> Yet, a moment since, I wish'd myself the milkmaid singing here, To kiss and cuff among the birds and flowers-- A right rough life and healthful </s>
<s> LADY </s>
<s> But the wench Hath her own troubles; she is weeping now; For the wrong Robin took her at her word </s>
<s> Then the cow kick'd, and all her milk was spilt </s>
<s> Your Highness such a milkmaid </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> I had kept My Robins and my cows in sweeter order Had I been such </s>
<s> LADY (_slyly_) </s>
<s> And had your Grace a Robin </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> Come, come, you are chill here; you want the sun That shines at court; make ready for the journey </s>
<s> Pray God, we 'scape the sunstroke </s>
<s> Ready at once </s>
<s> [_Exeunt_ </s>
<s> SCENE VI.--LONDON </s>
<s> A ROOM IN THE PALACE </s>
<s> LORD PETRE _and_ LORD WILLIAM HOWARD </s>
<s> PETRE </s>
<s> You cannot see the Queen </s>
<s> Renard denied her, Ev'n now to me </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> Their Flemish go-between And all-in-all </s>

<s> Mercy, that herb-of-grace, Flowers now but seldom </s>
<s> PETRE </s>
<s> Only now perhaps </s>
<s> Because the Queen hath been three days in tears For Philip's going--like the wild hedge-rose Of a soft winter, possible, not probable, However you have prov'n it </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> I must see her </s>
<s> _Enter_ RENARD </s>
<s> RENARD </s>
<s> My Lords, you cannot see her Majesty </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> Why then the King </s>
<s> for I would have him bring it Home to the leisure wisdom of his Queen, Before he go, that since these statutes past, Gardiner out-Gardiners Gardiner in his heat, Bonner cannot out-Bonner his own self-- Beast!--but they play with fire as children do, And burn the house </s>
<s> I know that these are breeding A fierce resolve and fixt heart-hate in men Against the King, the Queen, the Holy Father, The faith itself </s>

<s> RENARD </s>
<s> Not now </s>

<s> [_Exeunt_ PETRE _and_ HOWARD </s>
<s> _Enter_ PHILIP _(musing)_ PHILIP </s>
<s> She will not have Prince Philibert of Savoy, I talk'd with her in vain--says she will live And die true maid--a goodly creature too </s>
<s> Would _she_ had been the Queen </s>
<s> yet she must have him; She troubles England: that she breathes in England Is life and lungs to every rebel birth That passes out of embryo </s>
<s> Simon Renard </s>
<s> This Howard, whom they fear, what was he saying </s>
<s> RENARD </s>
<s> What your imperial father said, my liege, To deal with heresy gentlier </s>
<s> Gardiner burns, And Bonner burns; and it would seem this people Care more for our brief life in their wet land, Than yours in happier Spain </s>
<s> I told my Lord He should not vex her Highness; she would say These are the means God works with, that His church May flourish </s>
<s> PHILIP </s>
<s> Ay, sir, but in statesmanship To strike too soon is oft to miss the blow </s>
<s> Thou knowest I bad my chaplain, Castro, preach Against these burnings </s>
<s> RENARD </s>
<s> And the Emperor Approved you, and when last he wrote, declared His comfort in your Grace that you were bland And affable to men of all estates, In hope to charm them from their hate of Spain </s>
<s> PHILIP </s>
<s> In hope to crush all heresy under Spain </s>
<s> But, Renard, I am sicker staying here Than any sea could make me passing hence, Tho' I be ever deadly sick at sea </s>
<s> So sick am I with biding for this child </s>
<s> Is it the fashion in this clime for women To go twelve months in bearing of a child </s>
<s> The nurses yawn'd, the cradle gaped, they led Processions, chanted litanies, clash'd their bells, Shot off their lying cannon, and her priests Have preach'd, the fools, of this fair prince to come; Till, by St </s>
<s> James, I find myself the fool </s>
<s> Why do you lift your eyebrow at me thus </s>
<s> RENARD </s>
<s> I never saw your Highness moved till now </s>
<s> PHILIP </s>
<s> So weary am I of this wet land of theirs, And every soul of man that breathes therein </s>
<s> RENARD </s>
<s> My liege, we must not drop the mask before The masquerade is over-- PHILIP </s>
<s> --Have I dropt it </s>
<s> I have but shown a loathing face to you, Who knew it from the first </s>
<s> _Enter_ MARY </s>
<s> MARY (_aside_) </s>
<s> With Renard </s>
<s> Still Parleying with Renard, all the day with Renard, And scarce a greeting all the day for me-- And goes to-morrow </s>

<s> PHILIP (_to_ RENARD, _who advances to him_) </s>
<s> Well, sir, is there more </s>
<s> RENARD (_who has perceived the QUEEN_) </s>

<s> Ay </s>
<s> RENARD </s>

<s> PHILIP </s>

<s> She play the harlot </s>
<s> never </s>
<s> RENARD </s>
<s> No, sire, no, Not dream'd of by the rabidest gospeller </s>

<s> She came upon it, read it, and then rent it, With all the rage of one who hates a truth He cannot but allow </s>

<s> PHILIP </s>
<s> Ay, and then </s>

<s> For should her love when you are gone, my liege, Witness these papers, there will not be wanting Those that will urge her injury--should her love-- And I have known such women more than one-- Veer to the counterpoint, and jealousy Hath in it an alchemic force to fuse Almost into one metal love and hate,-- And she impress her wrongs upon her Council, And these again upon her Parliament-- We are not loved here, and would be then perhaps Not so well holpen in our wars with France, As else we might be--here she comes </s>
<s> _Enter_ MARY </s>
<s> MARY </s>

<s> You say true, Madam </s>

<s> ACT IV </s>
<s> SCENE I.--A ROOM IN THE PALACE </s>
<s> MARY, CARDINAL POLE </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> What have you there </s>
<s> POLE </s>
<s> So please your Majesty, A long petition from the foreign exiles To spare the life of Cranmer </s>
<s> Bishop Thirlby, And my Lord Paget and Lord William Howard, Crave, in the same cause, hearing of your Grace </s>
<s> Hath he not written himself--infatuated-- To sue you for his life </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> His life </s>
<s> Oh, no; Not sued for that--he knows it were in vain </s>
<s> But so much of the anti-papal leaven Works in him yet, he hath pray'd me not to sully Mine own prerogative, and degrade the realm By seeking justice at a stranger's hand Against my natural subject </s>
<s> King and Queen, To whom he owes his loyalty after God, Shall these accuse him to a foreign prince </s>
<s> Death would not grieve him more </s>
<s> I cannot be True to this realm of England and the Pope Together, says the heretic </s>
<s> POLE </s>
<s> And there errs; As he hath ever err'd thro' vanity </s>
<s> A secular kingdom is but as the body Lacking a soul; and in itself a beast </s>
<s> The Holy Father in a secular kingdom Is as the soul descending out of heaven Into a body generate </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> Write to him, then </s>
<s> POLE </s>
<s> I will </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> And sharply, Pole </s>
<s> POLE </s>
<s> Here come the Cranmerites </s>
<s> _Enter_ THIRLBY, LORD PAGET, LORD WILLIAM HOWARD </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> Health to your Grace </s>
<s> Good morrow, my Lord Cardinal; We make our humble prayer unto your Grace That Cranmer may withdraw to foreign parts, Or into private life within the realm </s>
<s> In several bills and declarations, Madam, He hath recanted all his heresies </s>
<s> PAGET </s>
<s> Ay, ay; if Bonner have not forged the bills </s>
<s> [_Aside_ </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> Did not More die, and Fisher </s>
<s> he must burn </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> He hath recanted, Madam </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> The better for him </s>
<s> He burns in Purgatory, not in Hell </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> Ay, ay, your Grace; but it was never seen That any one recanting thus at full, As Cranmer hath, came to the fire on earth </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> It will be seen now, then </s>
<s> THIRLBY </s>
<s> O Madam, Madam </s>
<s> I thus implore you, low upon my knees, To reach the hand of mercy to my friend </s>
<s> I have err'd with him; with him I have recanted </s>
<s> What human reason is there why my friend Should meet with lesser mercy than myself </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> My Lord of Ely, this </s>
<s> After a riot We hang the leaders, let their following go </s>
<s> Cranmer is head and father of these heresies, New learning as they call it; yea, may God Forget me at most need when I forget Her foul divorce--my sainted mother--No!-- HOWARD </s>
<s> Ay, ay, but mighty doctors doubted there </s>
<s> The Pope himself waver'd; and more than one Row'd in that galley--Gardiner to wit, Whom truly I deny not to have been Your faithful friend and trusty councillor </s>
<s> Hath not your Highness ever read his book </s>
<s> His tractate upon True Obedience, Writ by himself and Bonner </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> I will take Such order with all bad, heretical books That none shall hold them in his house and live, Henceforward </s>
<s> No, my Lord </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> Then never read it </s>
<s> The truth is here </s>
<s> Your father was a man Of such colossal kinghood, yet so courteous, Except when wroth, you scarce could meet his eye And hold your own; and were he wroth indeed, You held it less, or not at all </s>
<s> I say, Your father had a will that beat men down; Your father had a brain that beat men down-- POLE </s>
<s> Not me, my Lord </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> No, for you were not here; You sit upon this fallen Cranmer's throne; And it would more become you, my Lord Legate, To join a voice, so potent with her Highness, To ours in plea for Cranmer than to stand On naked self-assertion </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> All your voices Are waves on flint </s>
<s> The heretic must burn </s>
<s> HOWARD </s>
<s> Yet once he saved your Majesty's own life; Stood out against the King in your behalf </s>
<s> At his own peril </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> I know not if he did; And if he did I care not, my Lord Howard </s>
<s> My life is not so happy, no such boon, That I should spare to take a heretic priest's, Who saved it or not saved </s>
<s> Why do you vex me </s>
<s> PAGET </s>
<s> Yet to save Cranmer were to serve the Church, Your Majesty's I mean; he is effaced, Self-blotted out; so wounded in his honour, He can but creep down into some dark hole Like a hurt beast, and hide himself and die; But if you burn him,--well, your Highness knows The saying, 'Martyr's blood--seed of the Church' </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> Of the true Church; but his is none, nor will be </s>
<s> You are too politic for me, my Lord Paget </s>
<s> And if he have to live so loath'd a life, It were more merciful to burn him now </s>
<s> THIRLBY </s>
<s> O yet relent </s>
<s> O, Madam, if you knew him As I do, ever gentle, and so gracious, With all his learning-- MARY </s>
<s> Yet a heretic still </s>
<s> His learning makes his burning the more just </s>
<s> THIRLBY </s>
<s> So worshipt of all those that came across him; The stranger at his hearth, and all his house-- MARY </s>
<s> His children and his concubine, belike </s>
<s> THIRLBY </s>
<s> To do him any wrong was to beget A kindness from him, for his heart was rich, Of such fine mould, that if you sow'd therein The seed of Hate, it blossom'd Charity </s>

<s> Such weeds make dunghills gracious </s>

<s> SCENE II.--OXFORD </s>
<s> CRANMER IN PRISON </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> Last night, I dream'd the faggots were alight, And that myself was fasten'd to the stake, I And found it all a visionary flame, Cool as the light in old decaying wood; And then King Harry look'd from out a cloud, And bad me have good courage; and I heard An angel cry 'There is more joy in Heaven,'-- And after that, the trumpet of the dead </s>
<s> [_Trumpets without_ </s>
<s> Why, there are trumpets blowing now: what is it </s>
<s> _Enter_ FATHER COLE </s>
<s> COLE </s>
<s> Cranmer, I come to question you again; Have you remain'd in the true Catholic faith I left you in </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> In the true Catholic faith, By Heaven's grace, I am more and more confirm'd </s>
<s> Why are the trumpets blowing, Father Cole </s>
<s> COLE </s>
<s> Cranmer, it is decided by the Council That you to-day should read your recantation Before the people in St </s>
<s> Mary's Church </s>
<s> And there be many heretics in the town, Who loathe you for your late return to Rome, And might assail you passing through the street, And tear you piecemeal: so you have a guard </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> Or seek to rescue me </s>
<s> I thank the Council </s>
<s> COLE </s>
<s> Do you lack any money </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> Nay, why should I </s>
<s> The prison fare is good enough for me </s>
<s> COLE </s>
<s> Ay, but to give the poor </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> Hand it me, then </s>
<s> I thank you </s>
<s> COLE </s>
<s> For a little space, farewell; Until I see you in St </s>
<s> Mary's Church </s>
<s> [_Exit_ COLE </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> It is against all precedent to burn One who recants; they mean to pardon me </s>
<s> To give the poor--they give the poor who die </s>
<s> Well, burn me or not burn me I am fixt; It is but a communion, not a mass: A holy supper, not a sacrifice; No man can make his Maker--Villa Garcia </s>
<s> _Enter_ VILLA GARCIA </s>
<s> VILLA GARCIA </s>
<s> Pray you write out this paper for me, Cranmer </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> Have I not writ enough to satisfy you </s>
<s> VILLA GARCIA </s>
<s> It is the last </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> Give it me, then </s>
<s> [_He writes_ </s>
<s> VILLA GARCIA </s>
<s> Now sign </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> I have sign'd enough, and I will sign no more </s>
<s> VILLA GARCIA </s>
<s> It is no more than what you have sign'd already, The public form thereof </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> It may be so; I sign it with my presence, if I read it </s>
<s> VILLA GARCIA </s>
<s> But this is idle of you </s>
<s> Well, sir, well, You are to beg the people to pray for you; Exhort them to a pure and virtuous life; Declare the Queen's right to the throne; confess Your faith before all hearers; and retract That Eucharistic doctrine in your book </s>
<s> Will you not sign it now </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> No, Villa Garcia, I sign no more </s>
<s> Will they have mercy on me </s>
<s> VILLA GARCIA </s>
<s> Have you good hopes of mercy </s>
<s> So, farewell </s>
<s> [_Exit_ </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> Good hopes, not theirs, have I that I am fixt, Fixt beyond fall; however, in strange hours, After the long brain-dazing colloquies, And thousand-times recurring argument Of those two friars ever in my prison, When left alone in my despondency, Without a friend, a book, my faith would seem Dead or half-drown'd, or else swam heavily Against the huge corruptions of the Church, Monsters of mistradition, old enough To scare me into dreaming, 'what am I, Cranmer, against whole ages' </s>
<s> was it so, Or am I slandering my most inward friend, To veil the fault of my most outward foe-- The soft and tremulous coward in the flesh </s>
<s> O higher, holier, earlier, purer church, I have found thee and not leave thee any more </s>
<s> It is but a communion, not a mass-- No sacrifice, but a life-giving feast </s>
<s> (_Writes_.) So, so; this will I say--thus will I pray </s>
<s> [_Puts up the paper_ </s>
<s> _Enter_ BONNER </s>
<s> BONNER </s>
<s> Good day, old friend; what, you look somewhat worn; And yet it is a day to test your health Ev'n at the best: I scarce have spoken with you Since when?--your degradation </s>
<s> At your trial Never stood up a bolder man than you; You would not cap the Pope's commissioner-- Your learning, and your stoutness, and your heresy, Dumbfounded half of us </s>
<s> So, after that, We had to dis-archbishop and unlord, And make you simple Cranmer once again </s>
<s> The common barber dipt your hair, and I Scraped from your finger-points the holy oil; And worse than all, you had to kneel to _me_; Which was not pleasant for you, Master Cranmer </s>
<s> Now you, that would not recognise the Pope, And you, that would not own the Real Presence, Have found a real presence in the stake, Which frights you back into the ancient faith: And so you have recanted to the Pope </s>
<s> How are the mighty fallen, Master Cranmer </s>
<s> CRANMER </s>
<s> You have been more fierce against the Pope than I; But why fling back the stone he strikes me with </s>
<s> [_Aside_ </s>
<s> O Bonner, if I ever did you kindness-- Power hath been given you to try faith by fire-- Pray you, remembering how yourself have changed, Be somewhat pitiful, after I have gone, To the poor flock--to women and to children-- That when I was archbishop held with me </s>
<s> BONNER </s>

<s> PETERS </s>
<s> You saw him how he past among the crowd; And ever as he walk'd the Spanish friars Still plied him with entreaty and reproach: But Cranmer, as the helmsman at the helm Steers, ever looking to the happy haven Where he shall rest at night, moved to his death; And I could see that many silent hands Came from the crowd and met his own; and thus When we had come where Ridley burnt with Latimer, He, with a cheerful smile, as one whose mind Is all made up, in haste put off the rags They had mock'd his misery with, and all in white, His long white beard, which he had never shaven Since Henry's death, down-sweeping to the chain, Wherewith they bound him to the stake, he stood More like an ancient father of the Church, Than heretic of these times; and still the friars Plied him, but Cranmer only shook his head, Or answer'd them in smiling negatives; Whereat Lord Williams gave a sudden cry:-- 'Make short </s>
<s> make short' </s>
<s> and so they lit the wood </s>
<s> Then Cranmer lifted his left hand to heaven, And thrust his right into the bitter flame; And crying, in his deep voice, more than once, 'This hath offended--this unworthy hand' </s>
<s> So held it till it all was burn'd, before The flame had reach'd his body; I stood near-- Mark'd him--he never uttered moan of pain: He never stirr'd or writhed, but, like a statue, Unmoving in the greatness of the flame, Gave up the ghost; and so past martyr-like-- Martyr I may not call him--past--but whither </s>

<s> Nay, but, my Lord, he denied purgatory </s>
<s> PAGET </s>
<s> Why then to heaven, and God ha' mercy on him </s>

<s> PAGET </s>
<s> But your moan is useless now: Come out, my Lord, it is a world of fools </s>

<s> ACT V </s>
<s> SCENE I.--LONDON </s>
<s> HALL IN THE PALACE </s>
<s> QUEEN, SIR NICHOLAS HEATH </s>
<s> HEATH </s>

<s> It must be look'd to, If war should fall between yourself and France; Or you will lose your Calais </s>
<s> MARY </s>

<s> [_Exit_ HEATH </s>

<s> MARY (_admiringly_) </s>

<s> No, Madam, no </s>
<s> a candle in the sun Is all but smoke--a star beside the moon Is all but lost; your people will not crown me-- Your people are as cheerless as your clime; Hate me and mine: witness the brawls, the gibbets </s>

<s> _Enter_ CARDINAL POLE </s>
<s> (MARY _rises_.) MARY </s>
<s> Reginald Pole, what news hath plagued thy heart </s>
<s> What makes thy favour like the bloodless head Fall'n on the block, and held up by the hair </s>
<s> Philip?-- POLE </s>
<s> No, Philip is as warm in life As ever </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> Ay, and then as cold as ever </s>
<s> Is Calais taken </s>
<s> POLE </s>
<s> Cousin, there hath chanced A sharper harm to England and to Rome, Than Calais taken </s>
<s> Julius the Third Was ever just, and mild, and father-like; But this new Pope Caraffa, Paul the Fourth, Not only reft me of that legateship Which Julius gave me, and the legateship Annex'd to Canterbury--nay, but worse-- And yet I must obey the Holy Father, And so must you, good cousin;--worse than all, A passing bell toll'd in a dying ear-- He hath cited me to Rome, for heresy, Before his Inquisition </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> I knew it, cousin, But held from you all papers sent by Rome, That you might rest among us, till the Pope, To compass which I wrote myself to Rome, Reversed his doom, and that you might not seem To disobey his Holiness </s>
<s> POLE </s>
<s> He hates Philip; He is all Italian, and he hates the Spaniard; He cannot dream that _I_ advised the war; He strikes thro' me at Philip and yourself </s>
<s> Nay, but I know it of old, he hates me too; So brands me in the stare of Christendom A heretic </s>
<s> Now, even now, when bow'd before my time, The house half-ruin'd ere the lease be out; When I should guide the Church in peace at home, After my twenty years of banishment, And all my lifelong labour to uphold The primacy--a heretic </s>
<s> Long ago, When I was ruler in the patrimony, I was too lenient to the Lutheran, And I and learned friends among ourselves Would freely canvass certain Lutheranisms </s>
<s> What then, he knew I was no Lutheran </s>
<s> A heretic </s>
<s> He drew this shaft against me to the head, When it was thought I might be chosen Pope, But then withdrew it </s>
<s> In full consistory, When I was made Archbishop, he approved me </s>
<s> And how should he have sent me Legate hither, Deeming me heretic </s>
<s> and what heresy since </s>
<s> But he was evermore mine enemy, And hates the Spaniard--fiery-choleric, A drinker of black, strong, volcanic wines, That ever make him fierier </s>
<s> I, a heretic </s>
<s> Your Highness knows that in pursuing heresy I have gone beyond your late Lord Chancellor,-- He cried Enough </s>
<s> enough </s>
<s> before his death.-- Gone beyond him and mine own natural man (It was God's cause); so far they call me now, The scourge and butcher of their English church </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> Have courage, your reward is Heaven itself </s>
<s> POLE </s>
<s> They groan amen; they swarm into the fire Like flies--for what </s>
<s> no dogma </s>
<s> They know nothing; They burn for nothing </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> You have done your best </s>
<s> POLE </s>
<s> Have done my best, and as a faithful son, That all day long hath wrought his father's work, When back he comes at evening hath the door Shut on him by the father whom he loved, His early follies cast into his teeth, And the poor son turn'd out into the street To sleep, to die--I shall die of it, cousin </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> I pray you be not so disconsolate; I still will do mine utmost with the Pope </s>
<s> Poor cousin </s>
<s> Have not I been the fast friend of your life Since mine began, and it was thought we two Might make one flesh, and cleave unto each other As man and wife </s>
<s> POLE </s>
<s> Ah, cousin, I remember How I would dandle you upon my knee At lisping-age </s>
<s> I watch'd you dancing once With your huge father; he look'd the Great Harry, You but his cockboat; prettily you did it, And innocently </s>
<s> No--we were not made One flesh in happiness, no happiness here; But now we are made one flesh in misery; Our bridemaids are not lovely--Disappointment, Ingratitude, Injustice, Evil-tongue, Labour-in-vain </s>
<s> MARY </s>
<s> Surely, not all in vain </s>
<s> Peace, cousin, peace </s>
<s> I am sad at heart myself </s>
<s> POLE </s>

<s> Away </s>

<s> In Hampton Court My window look'd upon the corridor; And I was robing;--this poor throat of mine, Barer than I should wish a man to see it,-- When he we speak of drove the window back, And, like a thief, push'd in his royal hand; But by God's providence a good stout staff Lay near me; and you know me strong of arm; I do believe I lamed his Majesty's For a day or two, tho', give the Devil his due, I never found he bore me any spite </s>

<s> FIRST </s>

<s> What are you </s>
<s> THIRD </s>
<s> What am I </s>
<s> One who cries continually with sweat and tears to the Lord God that it would please Him out of His infinite love to break down all kingship and queenship, all priesthood and prelacy; to cancel and abolish all bonds of human allegiance, all the magistracy, all the nobles, and all the wealthy; and to send us again, according to His promise, the one King, the Christ, and all things in common, as in the day of the first church, when Christ Jesus was King </s>

<s> CECIL </s>
<s> Many points weather'd, many perilous ones, At last a harbour opens; but therein Sunk rocks--they need fine steering--much it is To be nor mad, nor bigot--have a mind-- Nor let Priests' talk, or dream of worlds to be, Miscolour things about her--sudden touches For him, or him--sunk rocks; no passionate faith-- But--if let be--balance and compromise; Brave, wary, sane to the heart of her--a Tudor School'd by the shadow of death--a Boleyn, too, Glancing across the Tudor--not so well </s>

<s> How is the good Queen now </s>
<s> ALICE </s>
<s> Away from Philip </s>
<s> Back in her childhood--prattling to her mother Of her betrothal to the Emperor Charles, And childlike--jealous of him again--and once She thank'd her father sweetly for his book Against that godless German </s>
<s> Ah, those days Were happy </s>
<s> It was never merry world In England, since the Bible came among us </s>
<s> CECIL </s>
<s> And who says that </s>
<s> ALICE </s>
<s> It is a saying among the Catholics </s>
<s> CECIL </s>
<s> It never will be merry world in England, Till all men have their Bible, rich and poor </s>
<s> ALICE </s>
<s> The Queen is dying, or you dare not say it </s>
<s> _Enter_ ELIZABETH </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> The Queen is dead </s>
<s> CECIL </s>
<s> Then here she stands </s>
<s> my homage </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> She knew me, and acknowledged me her heir, Pray'd me to pay her debts, and keep the Faith: Then claspt the cross, and pass'd away in peace </s>
<s> I left her lying still and beautiful, More beautiful than in life </s>
<s> Why would you vex yourself, Poor sister </s>
<s> Sir, I swear I have no heart To be your Queen </s>
<s> To reign is restless fence, Tierce, quart, and trickery </s>
<s> Peace is with the dead </s>
<s> Her life was winter, for her spring was nipt: And she loved much: pray God she be forgiven </s>
<s> CECIL </s>
<s> Peace with the dead, who never were at peace </s>
<s> Yet she loved one so much--I needs must say-- That never English monarch dying left England so little </s>
<s> ELIZABETH </s>
<s> But with Cecil's aid And others, if our person be secured From traitor stabs--we will make England great </s>
<s> _Enter_ PAGET, _and other_ LORDS OF THE COUNCIL, SIR RALPH BAGENHALL, _etc_ </s>
<s> LORDS </s>
<s> God save Elizabeth, the Queen of England </s>
<s> BAGENHALL </s>
<s> God save the Crown </s>
<s> the Papacy is no more </s>
<s> PAGET (_aside_) </s>
<s> Are we so sure of that </s>
<s> ACCLAMATION </s>
<s> God save the Queen </s>
<s> END OF QUEEN MARY </s>
<s> HAROLD: A DRAMA </s>
<s> TO HIS EXCELLENCY THE RIGHT HON </s>
<s> LORD LYTTON, VICEROY AND GOVERNOR-GENERAL OF INDIA </s>
<s> My Dear Lord Lytton,--After old-world records--such as the Bayeux tapestry and the Roman de Rou,--Edward Freeman's History of the Norman Conquest, and your father's Historical Romance treating of the same times, have been mainly helpful to me in writing this Drama </s>
<s> Your father dedicated his 'Harold' to my father's brother; allow me to dedicate my 'Harold' to yourself </s>
<s> A </s>
<s> TENNYSON </s>
<s> SHOW-DAY AT BATTLE ABBEY, 1876 </s>
<s> A garden here--May breath and bloom of spring-- The cuckoo yonder from an English elm Crying 'with my false egg I overwhelm The native nest:' and fancy hears the ring Of harness, and that deathful arrow sing, And Saxon battleaxe clang on Norman helm </s>
<s> Here rose the dragon-banner of our realm: Here fought, here fell, our Norman-slander'd king </s>
<s> O Garden blossoming out of English blood </s>
<s> O strange hate-healer Time </s>
<s> We stroll and stare Where might made right eight hundred years ago; Might, right </s>
<s> ay good, so all things make for good-- But he and he, if soul be soul, are where Each stands full face with all he did below </s>
<s> _DRAMATIS PERSONAE_ KING EDWARD THE CONFESSOR </s>
<s> STIGAND, _created Archbishop of Canterbury by the Antipope Benedict_ </s>
<s> ALDRED, _Archbishop of York_ </s>
<s> THE NORMAN BISHOP OF LONDON </s>

<s> WILLIAM RUFUS </s>
<s> WILLIAM MALET, _a Norman Noble_.[1] EDWIN, _Earl of Mercia, Son of Alfgar of Mercia_ MORCAR, _Earl of Northumbria after Tostig, Son of Alfgar of Mercia_ GAMEL, _a Northumbrian Thane_ </s>
