<s> SCENE I.--LONDON </s>
<s> THE KING'S PALACE </s>
<s> (_A comet seen through the open window_.) ALDWYTH, GAMEL, COURTIERS _talking together_ </s>
<s> FIRST COURTIER </s>
<s> Lo </s>
<s> there once more--this is the seventh night </s>
<s> Yon grimly-glaring, treble-brandish'd scourge Of England </s>
<s> SECOND COURTIER </s>
<s> Horrible </s>
<s> FIRST COURTIER </s>
<s> Look you, there's a star That dances in it as mad with agony </s>
<s> THIRD COURTIER </s>
<s> Ay, like a spirit in Hell who skips and flies To right and left, and cannot scape the flame </s>
<s> SECOND COURTIER </s>
<s> Steam'd upward from the undescendable Abysm </s>
<s> FIRST COURTIER </s>
<s> Or floated downward from the throne Of God Almighty </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>
<s> Gamel, son of Orm, What thinkest thou this means </s>
<s> GAMEL </s>
<s> War, my dear lady </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>
<s> Doth this affright thee </s>
<s> GAMEL </s>
<s> Mightily, my dear lady </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>
<s> Stand by me then, and look upon my face, Not on the comet </s>
<s> _Enter_ MORCAR </s>
<s> Brother </s>
<s> why so pale </s>
<s> MORCAR </s>
<s> It glares in heaven, it flares upon the Thames, The people are as thick as bees below, They hum like bees,--they cannot speak--for awe; Look to the skies, then to the river, strike Their hearts, and hold their babies up to it </s>
<s> I think that they would Molochize them too, To have the heavens clear </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>
<s> They fright not me </s>
<s> _Enter_ LEOFWIN, _after him_ GURTH </s>
<s> Ask thou Lord Leofwin what he thinks of this </s>
<s> MORCAR </s>
<s> Lord Leofwin, dost thou believe, that these Three rods of blood-red fire up yonder mean The doom of England and the wrath of Heaven </s>
<s> BISHOP OF LONDON (_passing_) </s>
<s> Did ye not cast with bestial violence Our holy Norman bishops down from all Their thrones in England </s>
<s> I alone remain </s>
<s> Why should not Heaven be wroth </s>
<s> LEOFWIN </s>
<s> With us, or thee </s>
<s> BISHOP OF LONDON </s>
<s> Did ye not outlaw your archbishop Robert, Robert of Jumieges--well-nigh murder him too </s>
<s> Is there no reason for the wrath of Heaven </s>
<s> LEOFWIN </s>
<s> Why then the wrath of Heaven hath three tails, The devil only one </s>
<s> [_Exit_ BISHOP OF LONDON </s>
<s> _Enter_ ARCHBISHOP STIGAND </s>
<s> Ask _our_ Archbishop </s>
<s> Stigand should know the purposes of Heaven </s>
<s> STIGAND </s>
<s> Not I </s>
<s> I cannot read the face of heaven; Perhaps our vines will grow the better for it </s>
<s> LEOFWIN (_laughing_) </s>
<s> He can but read the king's face on his coins </s>
<s> STIGAND </s>
<s> Ay, ay, young lord, _there_ the king's face is power </s>
<s> GURTH </s>
<s> O father, mock not at a public fear, But tell us, is this pendent hell in heaven A harm to England </s>
<s> STIGAND </s>
<s> Ask it of King Edward </s>
<s> And he may tell thee, _I_ am a harm to England </s>
<s> Old uncanonical Stigand--ask of _me_ Who had my pallium from an Antipope </s>
<s> Not he the man--for in our windy world What's up is faith, what's down is heresy </s>
<s> Our friends, the Normans, holp to shake his chair </s>
<s> I have a Norman fever on me, son, And cannot answer sanely... </s>
<s> What it means </s>
<s> Ask our broad Earl </s>
<s> [_Pointing to_ HAROLD, _who enters_ </s>
<s> HAROLD (_seeing_ GAMEL) </s>
<s> Hail, Gamel, son of Orm </s>
<s> Albeit no rolling stone, my good friend Gamel, Thou hast rounded since we met </s>
<s> Thy life at home Is easier than mine here </s>
<s> Look </s>
<s> am I not Work-wan, flesh-fallen </s>
<s> GAMEL </s>
<s> Art thou sick, good Earl </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Sick as an autumn swallow for a voyage, Sick for an idle week of hawk and hound Beyond the seas--a change </s>
<s> When camest thou hither </s>
<s> GAMEL </s>
<s> To-day, good Earl </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Is the North quiet, Gamel </s>
<s> GAMEL </s>
<s> Nay, there be murmurs, for thy brother breaks us With over-taxing--quiet, ay, as yet-- Nothing as yet </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Stand by him, mine old friend, Thou art a great voice in Northumberland </s>
<s> Advise him: speak him sweetly, he will hear thee </s>
<s> He is passionate but honest </s>
<s> Stand thou by him </s>
<s> More talk of this to-morrow, if yon weird sign Not blast us in our dreams.--Well, father Stigand-- [_To_ STIGAND, _who advances to him_ </s>
<s> STIGAND (_pointing to the comet_) </s>
<s> War there, my son </s>
<s> is that the doom of England </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Why not the doom of all the world as well </s>
<s> For all the world sees it as well as England </s>
<s> These meteors came and went before our day, Not harming any: it threatens us no more Than French or Norman </s>
<s> War </s>
<s> the worst that follows Things that seem jerk'd out of the common rut Of Nature is the hot religious fool, Who, seeing war in heaven, for heaven's credit Makes it on earth: but look, where Edward draws A faint foot hither, leaning upon Tostig </s>
<s> He hath learnt to love our Tostig much of late </s>
<s> LEOFWIN </s>
<s> And _he_ hath learnt, despite the tiger in him, To sleek and supple himself to the king's hand </s>
<s> GURTH </s>
<s> I trust the kingly touch that cures the evil May serve to charm the tiger out of him </s>
<s> LEOFWIN </s>
<s> He hath as much of cat as tiger in him </s>
<s> Our Tostig loves the hand and not the man </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Nay </s>
<s> Better die than lie </s>
<s> _Enter_ KING, QUEEN, _and_ TOSTIG </s>
<s> EDWARD </s>
<s> In heaven signs </s>
<s> Signs upon earth </s>
<s> signs everywhere </s>
<s> your Priests Gross, worldly, simoniacal, unlearn'd </s>
<s> They scarce can read their Psalter; and your churches Uncouth, unhandsome, while in Normanland God speaks thro' abler voices, as He dwells In statelier shrines </s>
<s> I say not this, as being Half Norman-blooded, nor as some have held, Because I love the Norman better--no, But dreading God's revenge upon this realm For narrowness and coldness: and I say it For the last time perchance, before I go To find the sweet refreshment of the Saints </s>
<s> I have lived a life of utter purity: I have builded the great church of Holy Peter: I have wrought miracles--to God the glory-- And miracles will in my name be wrought Hereafter.--I have fought the fight and go-- I see the flashing of the gates of pearl-- And it is well with me, tho' some of you Have scorn'd me--ay--but after I am gone Woe, woe to England </s>
<s> I have had a vision; The seven sleepers in the cave at Ephesus Have turn'd from right to left </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> My most dear Master, What matters </s>
<s> let them turn from left to right And sleep again </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> Too hardy with thy king </s>
<s> A life of prayer and fasting well may see Deeper into the mysteries of heaven Than thou, good brother </s>
<s> ALDWYTH (_aside_) </s>
<s> Sees he into thine, That thou wouldst have his promise for the crown </s>
<s> EDWARD </s>
<s> Tostig says true; my son, thou art too hard, Not stagger'd by this ominous earth and heaven: But heaven and earth are threads of the same loom, Play into one another, and weave the web That may confound thee yet </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Nay, I trust not, For I have served thee long and honestly </s>
<s> EDWARD </s>
<s> I know it, son; I am not thankless: thou Hast broken all my foes, lighten'd for me The weight of this poor crown, and left me time And peace for prayer to gain a better one </s>
<s> Twelve years of service </s>
<s> England loves thee for it </s>
<s> Thou art the man to rule her </s>
<s> ALDWYTH (_aside_) </s>
<s> So, not Tostig </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> And after those twelve years a boon, my king, Respite, a holiday: thyself wast wont To love the chase: thy leave to set my feet On board, and hunt and hawk beyond the seas </s>
<s> EDWARD </s>
<s> What, with this flaming horror overhead </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Well, when it passes then </s>
<s> EDWARD </s>
<s> Ay if it pass </s>
<s> Go not to Normandy--go not to Normandy </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> And wherefore not, my king, to Normandy </s>
<s> Is not my brother Wulfnoth hostage there For my dead father's loyalty to thee </s>
<s> I pray thee, let me hence and bring him home </s>
<s> EDWARD </s>
<s> Not thee, my son: some other messenger </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> And why not me, my lord, to Normandy </s>
<s> Is not the Norman Count thy friend and mine </s>
<s> EDWARD </s>
<s> I pray thee, do not go to Normandy </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Because my father drove the Normans out Of England?--That was many a summer gone-- Forgotten and forgiven by them and thee </s>
<s> EDWARD </s>
<s> Harold, I will not yield thee leave to go </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Why then to Flanders </s>
<s> I will hawk and hunt In Flanders </s>
<s> EDWARD </s>
<s> Be there not fair woods and fields In England </s>
<s> Wilful, wilful </s>
<s> Go--the Saints Pilot and prosper all thy wandering out And homeward </s>
<s> Tostig, I am faint again </s>
<s> Son Harold, I will in and pray for thee </s>
<s> [_Exit, leaning on_ TOSTIG, _and followed by_ STIGAND, MORCAR, _and_ COURTIERS </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> What lies upon the mind of our good king That he should harp this way on Normandy </s>
<s> QUEEN </s>
<s> Brother, the king is wiser than he seems; And Tostig knows it; Tostig loves the king </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> And love should know; and--be the king so wise,-- Then Tostig too were wiser than he seems </s>
<s> I love the man but not his phantasies </s>
<s> _Re-enter_ TOSTIG </s>
<s> Well, brother, When didst thou hear from thy Northumbria </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> When did I hear aught but this '_When_' from thee </s>
<s> Leave me alone, brother, with my Northumbria: She is _my_ mistress, let _me_ look to her </s>
<s> The King hath made me Earl; make me not fool </s>
<s> Nor make the King a fool, who made me Earl </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> No, Tostig--lest I make myself a fool Who made the King who made thee, make thee Earl </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> Why chafe me then </s>
<s> Thou knowest I soon go wild </s>
<s> GURTH </s>
<s> Come, come </s>
<s> as yet thou art not gone so wild But thou canst hear the best and wisest of us </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> So says old Gurth, not I: yet hear </s>
<s> thine earldom, Tostig, hath been a kingdom </s>
<s> Their old crown Is yet a force among them, a sun set But leaving light enough for Alfgar's house To strike thee down by--nay, this ghastly glare May heat their fancies </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> My most worthy brother, Thou art the quietest man in all the world-- Ay, ay and wise in peace and great in war-- Pray God the people choose thee for their king </s>
<s> But all the powers of the house of Godwin Are not enframed in thee </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Thank the Saints, no </s>
<s> But thou hast drain'd them shallow by thy tolls, And thou art ever here about the King: Thine absence well may seem a want of care </s>
<s> Cling to their love; for, now the sons of Godwin Sit topmost in the field of England, envy, Like the rough bear beneath the tree, good brother, Waits till the man let go </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> Good counsel truly </s>
<s> I heard from my Northumbria yesterday </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> How goes it then with thy Northumbria </s>
<s> Well </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> And wouldst thou that it went aught else than well </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> I would it went as well as with mine earldom, Leofwin's and Gurth's </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> Ye govern milder men </s>
<s> GURTH </s>
<s> We have made them milder by just government </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> Ay, ever give yourselves your own good word </s>
<s> LEOFWIN </s>
<s> An honest gift, by all the Saints, if giver And taker be but honest </s>
<s> but they bribe Each other, and so often, an honest world Will not believe them </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> I may tell thee, Tostig, I heard from thy Northumberland to-day </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> From spies of thine to spy my nakedness In my poor North </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> There is a movement there, A blind one--nothing yet </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> Crush it at once With all the power I have!--I must--I will!-- Crush it half-born </s>
<s> Fool still </s>
<s> or wisdom there, My wise head-shaking Harold </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Make not thou The nothing something </s>
<s> Wisdom when in power And wisest, should not frown as Power, but smile As kindness, watching all, till the true _must_ Shall make her strike as Power: but when to strike-- O Tostig, O dear brother--If they prance, Rein in, not lash them, lest they rear and run And break both neck and axle </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> Good again </s>
<s> Good counsel tho' scarce needed </s>
<s> Pour not water In the full vessel running out at top To swamp the house </s>
<s> LEOFWIN </s>
<s> Nor thou be a wild thing Out of the waste, to turn and bite the hand Would help thee from the trap </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> Thou playest in tune </s>
<s> LEOFWIN </s>
<s> To the deaf adder thee, that wilt not dance However wisely charm'd </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> No more, no more </s>
<s> GURTH </s>
<s> I likewise cry 'no more' </s>
<s> Unwholesome talk For Godwin's house </s>
<s> Leofwin, thou hast a tongue </s>
<s> Tostig, thou look'st as thou wouldst spring upon him </s>
<s> St </s>
<s> Olaf, not while I am by </s>
<s> Come, come, Join hands, let brethren dwell in unity; Let kith and kin stand close as our shield-wall, Who breaks us then </s>
<s> I say, thou hast a tongue, And Tostig is not stout enough to bear it </s>
<s> Vex him not, Leofwin </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> No, I am not vext,-- Altho' ye seek to vex me, one and all </s>
<s> I have to make report of my good earldom To the good king who gave it--not to you-- Not any of you.--I am not vext at all </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> The king </s>
<s> the king is ever at his prayers; In all that handles matter of the state I am the king </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> That shall thou never be If I can thwart thee </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Brother, brother </s>
<s> TOSTIG </s>
<s> Away </s>
<s> [_Exit_ TOSTIG </s>
<s> QUEEN </s>
<s> Spite of this grisly star ye three must gall Poor Tostig </s>
<s> LEOFWIN </s>
<s> Tostig, sister, galls himself; He cannot smell a rose but pricks his nose Against the thorn, and rails against the rose </s>
<s> QUEEN </s>
<s> I am the only rose of all the stock That never thorn'd him; Edward loves him, so Ye hate him </s>
<s> Harold always hated him </s>
<s> Why--how they fought when boys--and, Holy Mary </s>
<s> How Harold used to beat him </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Why, boys will fight </s>
<s> Leofwin would often fight me, and I beat him </s>
<s> Even old Gurth would fight </s>
<s> I had much ado To hold mine own against old Gurth </s>
<s> Old Gurth, We fought like great states for grave cause; but Tostig-- On a sudden--at a something--for a nothing-- The boy would fist me hard, and when we fought I conquer'd, and he loved me none the less, Till thou wouldst get him all apart, and tell him That where he was but worsted, he was wrong'd </s>
<s> Ah </s>
<s> thou hast taught the king to spoil him too; Now the spoilt child sways both </s>
<s> Take heed, take heed; Thou art the Queen; ye are boy and girl no more: Side not with Tostig in any violence, Lest thou be sideways guilty of the violence </s>
<s> QUEEN </s>
<s> Come fall not foul on me </s>
<s> I leave thee, brother </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Nay, my good sister-- [_Exeunt_ QUEEN, HAROLD, GURTH, _and_ LEOFWIN </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>
<s> Gamel, son of Orm, What thinkest thou this means </s>
<s> [_Pointing to the comet_ </s>
<s> GAMEL </s>
<s> War, my dear lady, War, waste, plague, famine, all malignities </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>
<s> It means the fall of Tostig from his earldom </s>
<s> GAMEL </s>
<s> That were too small a matter for a comet </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>
<s> It means the lifting of the house of Alfgar </s>
<s> GAMEL </s>
<s> Too small </s>
<s> a comet would not show for that </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>
<s> Not small for thee, if thou canst compass it </s>
<s> GAMEL </s>
<s> Thy love </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>
<s> As much as I can give thee, man; This Tostig is, or like to be, a tyrant; Stir up thy people: oust him </s>
<s> GAMEL </s>
<s> And thy love </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>
<s> As much as thou canst bear </s>
<s> GAMEL </s>
<s> I can bear all, And not be giddy </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>
<s> No more now: to-morrow </s>
<s> SCENE II.--IN THE GARDEN </s>
<s> THE KING'S HOUSE NEAR LONDON </s>
<s> SUNSET </s>
<s> EDITH </s>
<s> Mad for thy mate, passionate nightingale... </s>
<s> I love thee for it--ay, but stay a moment; _He_ can but stay a moment: he is going </s>
<s> I fain would hear him coming!.. </s>
<s> near me .. </s>
<s> near </s>
<s> Somewhere--To draw him nearer with a charm Like thine to thine </s>
<s> (_Singing_.) Love is come with a song and a smile, Welcome Love with a smile and a song: Love can stay but a little while </s>
<s> Why cannot he stay </s>
<s> They call him away: Ye do him wrong, ye do him wrong; Love will stay for a whole life long </s>
<s> _Enter_ HAROLD </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> The nightingales in Havering-at-the-Bower Sang out their loves so loud, that Edward's prayers Were deafen'd and he pray'd them dumb, and thus I dumb thee too, my wingless nightingale </s>

<s> _Enter_ ALDWYTH _from the thicket_ </s>
<s> ALDWYTH </s>

<s> I see the goal and half the way to it.-- Peace-lover is our Harold for the sake Of England's wholeness--so--to shake the North With earthquake and disruption--some division-- Then fling mine own fair person in the gap A sacrifice to Harold, a peace-offering, A scape-goat marriage--all the sins of both The houses on mine head--then a fair life And bless the Queen of England </s>

<s> SCENE II.--BAYEUX </s>
<s> PALACE </s>

<s> MALET </s>

<s> SCENE I.--THE KING'S PALACE </s>

<s> Then a great Angel past along the highest Crying 'the doom of England,' and at once He stood beside me, in his grasp a sword Of lightnings, wherewithal he cleft the tree From off the bearing trunk, and hurl'd it from him Three fields away, and then he dash'd and drench'd, He dyed, he soak'd the trunk with human blood, And brought the sunder'd tree again, and set it Straight on the trunk, that thus baptized in blood Grew ever high and higher, beyond my seeing, And shot out sidelong boughs across the deep That dropt themselves, and rooted in far isles Beyond my seeing: and the great Angel rose And past again along the highest crying 'The doom of England'!--Tostig, raise my head </s>

<s> SCENE II.--IN THE GARDEN </s>
<s> THE KING'S HOUSE NEAR LONDON </s>
<s> EDITH </s>
<s> Crown'd, crown'd and lost, crown'd King--and lost to me </s>
<s> (_Singing_.) Two young lovers in winter weather, None to guide them, Walk'd at night on the misty heather; Night, as black as a raven's feather; Both were lost and found together, None beside them </s>
<s> That is the burthen of it--lost and found Together in the cruel river Swale A hundred years ago; and there's another, Lost, lost, the light of day, To which the lover answers lovingly 'I am beside thee' </s>

<s> ACT V </s>
<s> SCENE I.--A TENT ON A MOUND, FROM WHICH CAN BE SEEN THE FIELD OF SENLAC </s>
<s> HAROLD, _sitting; by him standing_ HUGH MARGOT _the Monk_, GURTH, LEOFWIN, HAROLD </s>
<s> Refer my cause, my crown to Rome!.. </s>
<s> The wolf Mudded the brook and predetermined all </s>
<s> Monk, Thou hast said thy say, and had my constant 'No' For all but instant battle </s>
<s> I hear no more </s>
<s> MARGOT </s>
<s> Hear me again--for the last time </s>
<s> Arise, Scatter thy people home, descend the hill, Lay hands of full allegiance in thy Lord's And crave his mercy, for the Holy Father Hath given this realm of England to the Norman </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Then for the last time, monk, I ask again When had the Lateran and the Holy Father To do with England's choice of her own king </s>
<s> MARGOT </s>
<s> Earl, the first Christian Caesar drew to the East To leave the Pope dominion in the West He gave him all the kingdoms of the West </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> So!--did he?--Earl--I have a mind to play The William with thine eyesight and thy tongue </s>
<s> Earl--ay--thou art but a messenger of William </s>
<s> I am weary--go: make me not wroth with thee </s>
<s> MARGOT </s>
<s> Mock-king, I am the messenger of God, His Norman Daniel </s>
<s> Mene, Mene, Tekel </s>
<s> Is thy wrath Hell, that I should spare to cry, Yon heaven is wroth with _thee?_ Hear me again </s>
<s> Our Saints have moved the Church that moves the world, And all the Heavens and very God: they heard-- They know King Edward's promise and thine--thine </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Should they not know free England crowns herself </s>
<s> Not know that he nor I had power to promise </s>
<s> Not know that Edward cancell'd his own promise </s>
<s> And for my part therein--Back to that juggler, [_Rising_ </s>
<s> Tell him the saints are nobler than he dreams, Tell him that God is nobler than the Saints, And tell him we stand arm'd on Senlac Hill, And bide the doom of God </s>
<s> MARGOT </s>
<s> Hear it thro' me </s>
<s> The realm for which thou art forsworn is cursed, The babe enwomb'd and at the breast is cursed, The corpse thou whelmest with thine earth is cursed, The soul who fighteth on thy side is cursed, The seed thou sowest in thy field is cursed, The steer wherewith thou plowest thy field is cursed, The fowl that fleeth o'er thy field is cursed, And thou, usurper, liar-- HAROLD </s>
<s> Out, beast monk </s>
<s> [_Lifting his hand to strike him_ </s>
<s> GURTH _stops the blow_ </s>
<s> I ever hated monks </s>
<s> MARGOT </s>
<s> I am but a voice Among you: murder, martyr me if ye will-- HAROLD </s>
<s> Thanks, Gurth </s>
<s> The simple, silent, selfless man Is worth a world of tonguesters </s>
<s> (_To_ MARGOT.) Get thee gone </s>
<s> He means the thing he says </s>
<s> See him out safe </s>
<s> LEOFWIN </s>
<s> He hath blown himself as red as fire with curses </s>
<s> An honest fool </s>
<s> Follow me, honest fool, But if thou blurt thy curse among our folk, I know not--I may give that egg-bald head The tap that silences </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> See him out safe </s>
<s> [_Exeunt_ LEOFWIN _and_ MARGOT </s>
<s> GURTH </s>
<s> Thou hast lost thine even temper, brother Harold </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Gurth, when I past by Waltham, my foundation For men who serve the neighbour, not themselves, I cast me down prone, praying; and, when I rose, They told me that the Holy Rood had lean'd And bow'd above me; whether that which held it Had weaken'd, and the Rood itself were bound To that necessity which binds us down; Whether it bow'd at all but in their fancy; Or if it bow'd, whether it symbol'd ruin Or glory, who shall tell </s>
<s> but they were sad, And somewhat sadden'd me </s>
<s> GURTH </s>
<s> Yet if a fear, Or shadow of a fear, lest the strange Saints By whom thou swarest, should have power to balk Thy puissance in this fight with him, who made And heard thee swear--brother--_I_ have not sworn-- If the king fall, may not the kingdom fall </s>
<s> But if I fall, I fall, and thou art king; And, if I win, I win, and thou art king; Draw thou to London, there make strength to breast Whatever chance, but leave this day to me </s>
